“How’s she going to manage that?” asked Harry.

“She keeps trying to get **Tonks** round for dinner. I think she’s hoping **Bill** will fall for Tonks instead. I hope he does, I’d much rather have her in the family.”

“Yeah, that’ll work,” said Ron sarcastically. “Listen, no bloke in his right mind’s going to fancy Tonks when **Fleur**’s around. I mean, Tonks is okay-looking when she isn’t doing stupid things to her hair and her nose, but…”

“She’s a damn sight nicer than Phlegm,” said Ginny.

“And she’s more intelligent, she’s an **Auror**!” said Hermione from the corner.

“Fleur’s not stupid, she was good enough to enter the **Triwizard Tournament**,” said Harry.

“Not you as well!” said Hermione bitterly.

“I suppose you like the way Phlegm says ‘’Arry,’ do you?” asked Ginny scornfully.

“No,” said Harry, wishing he hadn’t spoken, “I was just saying, Phlegm… I mean, Fleur…”

“I’d much rather have Tonks in the family,” said Ginny. “At least she’s a laugh.”

“She hasn’t been much of a laugh lately,” said Ron. “Every time I’ve seen her she’s looked more like **Moaning Myrtle**.”

“That’s not fair,” snapped Hermione. “She still hasn’t got over what happened… you know… I mean, he was her cousin!”

Harry’s heart sank. They had arrived at **Sirius**.

---

## Tonks' Grief and Metamorphosis Difficulties

He picked up a fork and began shoveling scrambled eggs into his mouth, hoping to deflect any invitation to join in this part of the conversation.

“Tonks and Sirius barely knew each other!” said Ron. “Sirius was in **Azkaban** half her life and before that their families never met—”

“That’s not the point,” said Hermione. “She thinks it was her fault

## The Owls Delivering the O.W.L. Results

The **owls** were flying directly at the **Burrow**, three handsome **tawnies**, each carrying a large square envelope. As they flew lower, it became clear they were delivering important mail.

“Oh no!” squealed **Hermione**.

Mrs. Weasley opened the kitchen window, and all three owls soared in and landed on the table. Each lifted their right leg.

Harry moved forward and untied the letter addressed to him from the middle owl’s leg. Ron and Hermione struggled with their own letters. Hermione’s hands shook so much she made her owl tremble.

Nobody in the kitchen spoke as Harry opened his envelope and unfolded the parchment.

## Ordinary Wizarding Level Results

### Pass Grades

- **Outstanding (O)**
- **Exceeds Expectations (E)**
- **Acceptable (A)**

### Fail Grades

- **Poor (P)**
- **Dreadful (D)**
- **Troll (T)**

### Harry James Potter's Grades

- **Astronomy**: A  
- **Care of Magical Creatures**: E  
- **Charms**: E  
- **Defense Against the Dark Arts**: O  
- **Divination**: P  
- **Herbology**: E  
- **History of Magic**: D  
- **Potions**: E  
- **Transfiguration**: E  

Harry read the parchment several times, his breathing easing with each reading. He had always known he would fail **Divination** and had no chance in **History of Magic** due to collapsing during the exam. But he had passed everything else!

He passed well in **Transfiguration** and **Herbology**, exceeded expectations in **Potions**, and achieved **Outstanding** in **Defense Against the Dark Arts**.

Looking around, Hermione had her back to him, her head bent, but Ron looked delighted.

“Only failed Divination and History of Magic, and who cares about them?” said Ron happily. He asked to swap results, but had no **Outstandings**.

“Knew you’d be top at Defense Against the Dark Arts,” Ron said, punching Harry on the shoulder. “We’ve done all right, haven’t we?”

Mrs. Weasley ruffled Ron’s hair proudly. “Seven O.W.L.s, that’s more than Fred and George got together!”

Ginny asked Hermione about her results. Hermione said “Not bad” quietly.

Ron snatched Hermione’s results from her hand. She had **ten Outstandings** and one “Exceeds Expectations” in **Defense Against the Dark Arts**. Ron teased her about being disappointed, but Hermione only shook her head.

Harry laughed.

“Well, we’re **N.E.W.T.** students now!” grinned Ron. “Mum, are there any more sausages?”

Harry looked again at his results, as good as he could have hoped. He felt one tiny regret: his ambition to become an **Auror** ended because he did not have the required **Potions** grade. He had always known he wouldn’t pass Potions at the required standard, but the small black “E” still sank his stomach.

It was ironic that a **Death Eater** in disguise had told him he would make a good Auror, and the idea had taken hold. Since hearing the prophecy — "**Neither can live while the other survives**" — Harry felt fulfilling this destiny meant joining the highly trained wizards aiming to find and kill **Voldemort**.

---

## 6. DRACO’S DETOUR

Harry stayed within the Burrow’s garden for the next few weeks. He spent most days playing two-a-side **Quidditch** games in the Weasleys’ orchard: Harry and Hermione against Ron and Ginny. Hermione was dreadful, Ginny good, making the teams fairly even.

Evenings were spent eating triple helpings of everything Mrs. Weasley cooked.

The holiday would have been happy and peaceful if not for the constant **disappearances**, **accidents**, and even **deaths** appearing almost daily in the **Daily Prophet**. Bill and Mr. Weasley often brought home news before it reached the paper.

Harry’s sixteenth birthday celebrations were marred by grim news, brought by **Remus Lupin**, looking gaunt, grim, and with gray-streaked hair.

“There have been another couple of **Dementor attacks**,” Lupin announced, as Mrs. Weasley passed him cake. His tone was heavy.

They had found **Igor Karkaroff’s** body in a shack up north, marked with the **Dark Mark**. Lupin expressed surprise he lasted a year after deserting the Death Eaters. He mentioned Sirius’s brother **Regulus** only survived days after desertion.

Mrs. Weasley tried to change the subject.

Bill mentioned to Lupin the fate of **Florean Fortescue**, the man who ran the ice-cream place in **Diagon Alley**.

Harry interrupted, remembering the free ice creams Fortescue gave him, and asked what had happened.

“He was dragged off,” Bill said grimly.

Ron asked why, but Mrs. Weasley glared at Bill.

Mr. Weasley added that **Ollivander**, the wandmaker, was missing. His shop was empty, no signs of struggle, and no one knew if he left voluntarily or was kidnapped.

Ginny was startled: “But what’ll people do for wands?”

“They’ll make do with other makers,” Lupin said, “but Ollivander was the best. If the other side has got him, it’s bad for us.”

### Upcoming Trip to Diagon Alley

The day after the bleak birthday, Hogwarts letters and booklists arrived. Harry’s included a surprise: he had been made **Quidditch Captain**.

Hermione was excited: “That gives you equal status with prefects! You can use our special bathroom now!”

Ron was thrilled examining the Captain’s badge and joked about being let back on the team.

Mrs. Weasley checked Ron’s booklist and planned a trip to **Diagon Alley** for Saturday, provided Mr. Weasley didn’t have to work.

Ron joked about You-Know-Who hiding in the shops, which angered Mrs. Weasley. She reminded him about the seriousness of security after recent kidnappings.

Ron quickly said he wanted to come along to see **Fred and George’s** shop, and Mrs. Weasley warned him to behave or be left behind.

Ron stared at Harry incredulously as Mrs. Weasley left the room carrying a laundry basket and balancing a precarious clock.

He muttered, “Blimey… you can’t even make a joke round here anymore…”

Ron was careful not to be flippant about **Voldemort** over the next few days. The next Saturday dawned without Mrs. Weasley’s outbursts, but she seemed tense at breakfast.

Bill handed Harry a full money bag.

“Where’s mine?” Ron demanded.

Bill said it was already Harry’s and explained he withdrew it from Harry’s vault due to goblin security tightening after an incident involving **Arkie Philpott** and a **Probity Probe**.

Fleur praised Bill’s thoughtfulness, while Ginny mimed vomiting into her cereal. Harry choked, and Ron thumped him on the back.

### The Ministry Car and Security

It was an overcast day. A **Ministry of Magic** car awaited them in the yard. Harry had ridden once before.

Ron appreciated that Dad could get them the car again.

Harry, Ron, Hermione, and Ginny sat comfortably in the back seat.

Mr. Weasley sat up front with Mrs. Weasley and the Ministry driver. Mr. Weasley explained the high-grade security status Harry had been given and that more security would join them at **The Leaky Cauldron**.

Harry did not look forward to shopping surrounded by Aurors. He stowed his **Invisibility Cloak** in his backpack, thinking if it was good enough for **Dumbledore**, it should be good enough for the Ministry.

At **The Leaky Cauldron**, they were greeted, but there were no Aurors outside. Instead, **Rubeus Hagrid**, the Hogwarts gamekeeper, stood beaming.

“Harry!” Hagrid boomed, sweeping him into a bone-crushing hug. He talked enthusiastically about **Buckbeak — Witherwings**, who was happy to be back in the open air.

Harry joked about security meaning Hagrid’s presence.

Hagrid explained the Ministry wanted to send Aurors, but Dumbledore insisted he should come.

They entered the Leaky Cauldron, which was empty except for **Tom**, the wizened, toothless landlord.

Hagrid told Tom they were just passing through for Hogwarts business.

Tom nodded gloomily and returned to wiping glasses.

The group walked through the bar into the chilly courtyard. Hagrid raised his pink umbrella and rapped a brick in the wall, which opened to reveal an archway to a winding cobbled street.

They paused, looking around.

## Diagon Alley Changes

Diagon Alley had changed. The colorful, glittering window displays of **spellbooks, potion ingredients, and cauldrons** were lost to view, hidden behind large **Ministry of Magic posters**. Most of these somber purple posters carried blown-up versions of the **security advice** from Ministry pamphlets sent out over the summer, while others bore moving black-and-white photographs of **Death Eaters** known to be on the loose.

**Bellatrix Lestrange** sneered from the front of the nearest apothecary. A few windows, including those of **Florean Fortescue’s Ice Cream Parlor**, were boarded up. Meanwhile, shabby-looking stalls had sprung up along the street.

The nearest stall, outside **Flourish and Blotts** under a striped, stained awning, had a cardboard sign pinned to the front:

**AMULETS**  
Effective Against **Werewolves, Dementors, and Inferi!**

A seedy-looking wizard rattled armfuls of silver symbols on chains at the passersby.

---

## The Weasley Family's Shopping

- The amulet seller leered at **Mrs. Weasley and Ginny**, offering protection amulets.
- **Mr. Weasley** glared angrily but was restrained by **Mrs. Weasley** who nervously consulted a list.
- Mrs. Weasley wanted to visit **Madam Malkin’s** first for new dress robes as **Hermione** needed some, and **Ron** showed much too much ankle.
- Mr. Weasley suggested a split: the three children go with **Hagrid** to Madam Malkin’s, while he and Mrs. Weasley took Ginny to get schoolbooks at **Flourish and Blotts**.
- Mrs. Weasley was anxious but consented. Hagrid reassured her.

Shoppers moved with a harried, anxious look. Nobody stopped to talk anymore, sticking closely to their groups.

---

## Madam Malkin’s Shop Encounter

- Hagrid worried about the crowd but offered to stand guard outside.
- On entering, Harry, Ron, and Hermione heard a familiar voice: **Draco Malfoy** was present, trying on dark green robes.
- Malfoy insulted Hermione by calling her a "**Mudblood**."
- **Madam Malkin** admonished Malfoy to stop the language and warned no wands were allowed.
- Harry and Ron pointed their wands defensively but were told to put them away by **Narcissa Malfoy**, Draco’s mother.
- Narcissa threatened Harry, warning him not to attack her son again.
- Harry mockingly challenged Narcissa’s threats, hinting at **Death Eaters** and **Azkaban**.
- Draco tried to attack but stumbled; **Ron** laughed.
- Narcissa declared they would shop elsewhere and left, making a point of bumping Ron.

---

## After Malfoy’s Departure

- Madam Malkin hurried to dismiss the disruption and quickly fitted robes for Ron and Harry.
- She tried to sell Hermione wizard’s robes by mistake.
- She was glad to see the group leave.

---

## Rejoining the Weasleys

- Hagrid was unconcerned about the Malfoys causing trouble in Diagon Alley.
- The Weasleys returned with heavy packages of books.
- Mrs. Weasley planned to stop at the **Apothecary** and **Eeylops Owl Emporium** on the way to **Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes**, the joke shop run by **Fred and George**.

---

## The Visit to Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes

- Mrs. Weasley was concerned about time, eager to finish quickly and return to the car.
- The twins’ shop windows were vibrant and eye-catching amid dull poster-covered shops.
- The left window dazzled with revolving, popping, flashing, bouncing, and shrieking goods.
- The right window featured a flashing purple poster with yellow letters:

> WHY ARE YOU WORRYING ABOUT YOU-KNOW-WHO?  
> YOU SHOULD BE WORRYING ABOUT U-NO-POO—  
> THE CONSTIPATION SENSATION THAT’S GRIPPING THE NATION!

- Harry laughed at the poster; Mrs. Weasley silently mouthed "U-No-Poo," distressed.
- Ron found the joke brilliant and led the way into the crowded shop.

---

## Inside the Joke Shop

- Harry saw shelves piled high with products:
  - **Skiving Snackboxes**, perfected by Fred and George during their last year at Hogwarts.
  - The most popular being **Nosebleed Nougat**, with only one battered box left.
  - Bins of **trick wands** ranging from rubber chickens to aggressive ones.
  - Boxes of **quills**: Self-Inking, Spell-Checking, and Smart-Answer varieties.
- A crowd of ten-year-olds watched a **tiny wooden man** ascending gallows with the caption:  
  "**Reusable hangman—spell it or he’ll swing!**"
- Hermione examined a box of "**Patented Daydream Charms**" featuring a pirate ship scene.

---

## Daydream Charms Description

- According to the box information:
  - One simple incantation grants a **top-quality, highly realistic thirty-minute daydream**.
  - Easy to fit into an average school lesson and virtually undetectable.
  - Side effects include a **vacant expression** and **minor drooling**.
  - Not for sale to under-sixteens.
- Hermione remarked to Harry that this was "extraordinary magic."

---

## Encounter with Fred Weasley

- Fred appeared, wearing **magenta robes**, clashing with his flaming hair.
- He greeted Harry and asked about **Hermione’s black eye**.
- Hermione explained it was caused by a **punching telescope**.
- Fred produced a tub of thick yellow paste, promising the bruise would heal in an hour.
- Fred explained they tested most products on themselves.
- Hermione nervously asked if it was safe.

## Fred and George’s Joke Shop Tour

**Fred** braced himself and said, “’Course it is. Come on, Harry, I’ll give you a tour.” Harry left **Hermione** dabbing her black eye with paste and followed Fred toward the back of the shop. There, he saw a stand of **card and rope tricks**.

**Fred** happily pointed out, “Muggle magic tricks! For freaks like Dad, you know, who love Muggle stuff. It’s not a big earner, but we do fairly steady business, they’re great novelties…” He spotted **George**, who shook Harry’s hand energetically.

George warned a small boy who tried to pocket something from a tub labeled **Edible Dark Marks—They’ll Make Anyone Sick!** that he’d pay more than **Galleons** if caught.

## The Serious Product Line

George pushed back a curtain to reveal a darker, less crowded room with more subdued packaging.

- “We've just developed this more serious line,” said **Fred**.
- “Many people, even working at the Ministry, can’t do a decent **Shield Charm**,” added George.
- “The **Shield Hat** was a joke product, but the Ministry bought five hundred for its support staff! We’re getting massive orders.”

They expanded into a range including:

- **Shield Cloaks**
- **Shield Gloves**

“These wouldn’t help much against the Unforgivable Curses, but for minor to moderate hexes or jinxes...” Fred explained.

Wanting to capitalize on **Defense Against the Dark Arts**, George showed Harry new products:

- **Instant Darkness Powder** imported from **Peru**, ideal for quick escapes.
- **Decoy Detonators**, quirky black horn-like objects that create loud noises for diversions.

Harry caught a couple of Detonators from George, impressed by their usefulness.

## Customer Interaction and Specials

A young witch named **Verity**, wearing magenta staff robes, called for the Weasley twins from outside the curtain. Fred and George took it in stride despite being called “Mr. Weasley.”

George told Harry to take whatever he wanted, saying, “No charge” because Harry had given them a **start-up loan**.

Fred and George returned to the main shop, where Hermione and Ginny were examining **Patented Daydream Charms**.

## WonderWitch Product Range

Fred proudly introduced a cluster of excited girls to their special **WonderWitch** products near the window, including a violent pink range of **love potions**.

- Ginny skeptically asked, “Do they work?”
- Fred said they last up to **twenty-four hours**, depending on the boy's weight and the girl’s attractiveness.
- George warned they were not selling them to their sister, warning about her many admirers.

Ginny questioned Fred about a **ten-second pimple vanisher** and then asked about cute balls of fluff in a cage.

- “Pygmy Puffs,” said George. They were miniature **puffskeins** that couldn’t be bred fast enough.
- Ginny admitted she had dumped **Michael Corner** for being a bad loser.
  
Fred teased Ginny about her rapidly changing boyfriends, but Ginny shot a sharp, Mrs. Weasley-like glare.

## Ron’s Encounter and Mrs. Weasley’s Warning

Ron appeared, laden with merchandise. 

- Fred told him the total: **Three Galleons, nine Sickles, and a Knut.**
- Ron protested, but Fred insisted he pay for the items or put them back correctly.
- Ron made a rude gesture which Mrs. Weasley spotted.
- Mrs. Weasley sharply warned him she’d **jinx his fingers together** if he did it again.

Ginny immediately asked for a **Pygmy Puff**, exciting Mrs. Weasley.

## Draco Malfoy’s Mysterious Behavior

As Mrs. Weasley and Ginny looked at Pygmy Puffs, Harry, Ron, and Hermione noticed **Draco Malfoy** hurrying down the street alone. He glanced over his shoulder before disappearing.

- Harry suspected **Narcissa Malfoy** would never let Draco out alone willingly.
- They deduced Malfoy had escaped her control for some unknown reason.

## Using the Invisibility Cloak

Harry pulled out his **Invisibility Cloak** and urged Hermione and Ron to get under it.

- Hermione hesitated but eventually ducked under with Harry and Ron.
- They quietly left the shop unnoticed.

Malfoy had disappeared, apparently heading toward **Knockturn Alley**.

## Spy Mission in Knockturn Alley

The trio hurried after Malfoy but noticed Knockturn Alley was deserted, likely because buying **Dark Arts artifacts** was suspicious in dangerous times.

Hermione pointed out Malfoy entering a shop, **Borgin and Burkes**.

Inside, Malfoy was speaking animatedly with the sinister shop owner **Mr. Borgin**, who appeared fearful and resentful.

## Eavesdropping with Extendable Ears

Ron used **Extendable Ears** to eavesdrop on their conversation by feeding long strings under the door.

Transcript highlights:

- Malfoy asked Borgin if he could fix “it.”
- Borgin said he’d need to see the item, but Malfoy insisted it couldn’t be moved.
- Borgin was uneasy and uncertain about repairing the item.

Malfoy sneered and threatened Borgin:

- “Tell anyone, and there will be retribution.”
- He mentioned **Fenrir Greyback**, a family friend who would ensure Borgin cooperated.
- Borgin bowed deeply and agreed to keep quiet.

Malfoy instructed Borgin not to sell the item and warned, “Not a word to anyone, not even my mother.”

## Summary

The scene reveals the **Weasley twins’ joke shop** with its playful and serious product lines, interactions with customers and family, and Harry’s suspicion about Malfoy’s secretive visit to Borgin and Burkes, something potentially dangerous involving **Fenrir Greyback**.

## Scene at Borgin and Burkes

Next moment, the bell over the door tinkled loudly as **Malfoy stalked out of the shop** looking very pleased with himself. He passed so close to **Harry**, **Ron**, and **Hermione** that they felt the **cloak flutter** around their knees again. Inside the shop, **Borgin remained frozen**; his unctuous smile had vanished; he looked worried.

**Ron** whispered, "What was that about?" while reeling in the **Extendable Ears**.

**Harry** thought hard: "He wants something mended… and he wants to reserve something in there… Could you see what he pointed at when he said ‘that one’?"

“No, he was behind that cabinet…” said Ron.

“You two stay here,” whispered Hermione.

Hermione quickly ducked out from under the cloak, checked her hair in the glass reflection, then marched into the shop, setting the bell tinkling again. Ron hastily fed the **Extendable Ears** back under the door and passed one of the strings to Harry.

### Interaction with Mr. Borgin

Hermione greeted Borgin brightly: “Hello, horrible morning, isn’t it?” but Borgin only cast a suspicious look and said nothing.

She strolled through the jumble of objects on display.

- Asked if a **necklace** was for sale. Borgin said, “If you’ve got one and a half thousand **Galleons**.”
- Inquired about a **skull**. Borgin priced it at **sixteen Galleons**.
- Checked if items were reserved for anyone; Borgin squinted suspiciously.

Hermione suddenly blurted out a story:

> “The boy who was in here just now, Draco Malfoy, is a friend of mine. I want to get him a birthday present, but if he’s already reserved anything, I don’t want to get him the same thing…”

Borgin’s response was sharp:

> “Out. Get out!”

Hermione left quickly, Borgin following her to the door. He slammed it and put up the closed sign.

Ron remarked, “Worth a try, but you were a bit obvious…”

Hermione snapped back, “Well, next time you can show me how it’s done, Master of Mystery!”

### Return to Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes

Ron and Hermione bickered as they hurried back to **Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes**, needing to dodge an anxious **Mrs. Weasley** and **Hagrid** who had clearly noticed their absence.

Inside the shop, Harry removed the **Invisibility Cloak**, hid it in his bag, and joined the others as they insisted, in response to Mrs. Weasley’s accusations, that they had been in the back room all along.

---

## 7. THE SLUG CLUB

Harry spent most of the last week of the holidays pondering **Malfoy’s behavior in Knockturn Alley**. The most disturbing thing was the **satisfied look on Malfoy’s face** as he left the shop. Nothing that made Malfoy so happy could be good news.

To Harry’s annoyance, **Ron** and **Hermione** seemed less curious and bored of discussing it after a few days.

### Conversations about Malfoy

- Hermione, sitting on Fred and George’s windowsill, said impatiently there could be many explanations.
- Ron vaguely suggested maybe Malfoy’s **Hand of Glory** was broken.
- Harry countered that Malfoy said, *“Don’t forget to keep that one safe,”* implying Borgin had another broken object, possibly a pair.
- Harry believed Malfoy might be seeking **revenge** because his father was in **Azkaban**.
- Ron laughed at the idea of Malfoy seeking revenge or joining the **Death Eaters** at sixteen.
- Hermione also doubted Malfoy would be allowed to join.

Harry explained an important detail:

> “In Madam Malkin’s, Malfoy jerked his left arm away when she tried to roll up his sleeve. He’s been branded with the **Dark Mark**.”

Ron and Hermione exchanged skeptical looks.

Harry pressed on:

> “Malfoy showed Borgin something we couldn’t see. It seriously scared Borgin. It was the Dark Mark. Borgin took him very seriously!”

Ron and Hermione were still unsure.

Frustrated but convinced, Harry left the room with a pile of filthy **Quidditch robes**. Mrs. Weasley had urged them to finish their washing and packing early.

---

## Preparations for Departure

On the landing, Harry met **Ginny**, who warned him about **Phlegm** on the kitchen floor.

In the kitchen, **Fleur** was planning her wedding to **Bill** while Mrs. Weasley looked bad-tempered over some self-peeling sprouts.

- Fleur considered bridesmaid dresses in **pale gold** rather than **pink**.
- Mrs. Weasley explained Ministry security arrangements for their Hogwarts journey, mentioning **Aurors** at the station.
- Tonks would not be present this year.
- Mrs. Weasley urged Harry to finish packing trunks early to avoid a last-minute scramble.

### The Next Morning: Departure

- Ministry cars arrived to pick them up, with trunks packed, cats and pets safely enclosed.
- Fleur kissed Harry good-bye; Ron was embarrassed after falling in the dust at her feet.
- No **Hagrid** at King’s Cross; instead, two grim-faced Aurors escorted them.
- Mrs. Weasley seemed flustered by the efficient security.
- An Auror tried to guide Harry through the barrier, but Harry forced his way to **Platform 9¾**, boarding the **Hogwarts Express**.
- Hermione and the Weasleys followed quickly.
- Ron and Hermione had to go to the prefects' carriage first to patrol the corridors.

Mrs. Weasley wished Ron a lovely term.

---

## Harry's Private Conversation with Mr. Weasley

Harry asked Mr. Weasley for a quick word away from the group, trusting him because he worked at the **Ministry** and was less likely to overreact.

Mr. Weasley guessed they hadn’t been in the back room of Fred and George’s.

Harry admitted, “We followed Draco Malfoy using my Invisibility Cloak because I thought he was up to something. He slipped away from his mother.”

Harry explained:

- Malfoy went into Borgin and Burkes.
- He was bullying Borgin to fix something and reserve another item.
- Malfoy seemed to want a **pair** of objects fixed/reserved.
- Malfoy flinched when Madam Malkin touched his left arm; Harry suspected the **Dark Mark brand**.
- Harry believed Malfoy replaced his father as a **Death Eater**.

Mr. Weasley looked taken aback and replied:

> “Harry, I doubt whether You-Know-Who would allow a sixteen-year-old—”

## Dialogue and Investigation

“Does anyone really know what **You-Know-Who** would or wouldn’t do?” asked **Harry** angrily. 

“Mr. Weasley, I’m sorry, but isn’t it worth investigating? If **Malfoy** wants something fixing, and he needs to threaten **Borgin** to get it done, it’s probably something **Dark** or dangerous, isn’t it?”

“I doubt it, to be honest, Harry,” said **Mr. Weasley** slowly. “You see, when **Lucius Malfoy** was arrested, we raided his house. We took away everything that might have been dangerous.”

“I think you missed something,” said **Harry** stubbornly.

“Well, maybe,” said **Mr. Weasley**, but Harry could tell that Mr. Weasley was humoring him.

There was a whistle behind them; nearly everyone had boarded the train and the doors were closing.

“You’d better hurry!” said **Mr. Weasley**, as **Mrs. Weasley** cried, “Harry, quickly!”

---

## Boarding the Train

He hurried forward and **Mr. and Mrs. Weasley** helped him load his trunk onto the train.

“Now, dear, you’re coming to us for **Christmas**, it’s all fixed with **Dumbledore**, so we’ll see you quite soon,” said **Mrs. Weasley** through the window, as **Harry** slammed the door shut behind him and the train began to move.

“You make sure you look after yourself and—”

The train was gathering speed.

“—be good and—”

She was jogging to keep up now.

“—stay safe!”

Harry waved until the train had turned a corner and **Mr. and Mrs. Weasley** were lost to view, then turned to see where the others had got to.

He supposed **Ron** and **Hermione** were cloistered in the prefects’ carriage, but **Ginny** was a little way along the corridor, chatting to some friends.

He made his way toward her, dragging his trunk.

---

## Staring and Gossip on the Train

People stared shamelessly as he approached. They even pressed their faces against the windows of their compartments to get a look at him.

He had expected an upswing in the amount of gaping and gawping he would have to endure this term after all the “**Chosen One**” rumors in the **Daily Prophet**, but he did not enjoy the sensation of standing in a very bright spotlight.

He tapped **Ginny** on the shoulder.

“Fancy trying to find a compartment?”

“I can’t, Harry, I said I’d meet **Dean**,” said **Ginny** brightly. “See you later.”

“Right,” said Harry. He felt a strange twinge of annoyance as she walked away, her long red hair dancing behind her; he had become so used to her presence over the summer that he had almost forgotten that **Ginny** did not hang around with him, **Ron**, and **Hermione** while at school.

Then he blinked and looked around: He was surrounded by mesmerized girls.

---

## Meeting Neville and Luna

“Hi, Harry!” said a familiar voice from behind him.

“**Neville**!” said Harry in relief, turning to see a round-faced boy struggling toward him.

“Hello, Harry,” said a girl with long hair and large misty eyes, who was just behind **Neville**.

“**Luna**, hi, how are you?”

“Very well, thank you,” said **Luna**. She was clutching a magazine to her chest; large letters on the front announced that there was a pair of free **Spectrespecs** inside.

“The **Quibbler** still going strong, then?” asked Harry, who felt a certain fondness for the magazine, having given it an exclusive interview the previous year.

“Oh yes, circulation’s well up,” said Luna happily.

“Let’s find seats,” said Harry, and the three of them set off along the train through hordes of silently staring students.

At last they found an empty compartment, and Harry hurried inside gratefully.

---

## Talking in the Compartment

“They’re even staring at us,” said Neville, indicating himself and Luna. “Because we’re with you!”

“They’re staring at you because you were at the **Ministry** too,” said Harry, as he hoisted his trunk into the luggage rack. “Our little adventure there was all over the **Daily Prophet**; you must’ve seen it.”

“Yes, I thought **Gran** would be angry about all the publicity,” said Neville, “but she was really pleased. Says I’m starting to live up to my dad at long last. She bought me a new wand, look!”

He pulled it out and showed it to Harry.

“**Cherry** and **unicorn hair**,” he said proudly. “We think it was one of the last **Ollivander** ever sold, he vanished next day… oi, come back here, **Trevor**!”

And he dived under the seat to retrieve his toad as it made one of its frequent bids for freedom.

---

## Questioning About D.A. Meetings

“Are we still doing **D.A. meetings** this year, Harry?” asked **Luna**, who was detaching a pair of psychedelic spectacles from the middle of **The Quibbler**.

“No point now we’ve got rid of **Umbridge**, is there?” said Harry, sitting down

## Slughorn’s Lunch Gathering on the Train

Neville nodded, looking scared. At a gesture from **Slughorn**, they sat down opposite each other in the only two empty seats, which were nearest the door. Harry glanced around at their fellow guests.

He recognized a **Slytherin** from their year, a tall black boy with high cheekbones and long, slanting eyes. There were also two seventh-year boys Harry did not know and, squashed in the corner beside Slughorn and looking unsure, **Ginny**.

### Introductions by Slughorn

“Now, do you know everyone?” Slughorn asked Harry and Neville.

- **Blaise Zabini**: In their year but showed no sign of recognition or greeting.
- **Cormac McLaggen**: A large, wiry-haired youth; Harry and Neville nodded back at him.
- **Marcus Belby**: Thin and nervous-looking, gave a strained smile.
- The “charming young lady” who knew them: **Ginny**, grimacing from behind Slughorn’s back.

Slughorn welcomed them, offering lunch and conversations about well-known family connections:

- **Belby’s** Uncle **Damocles**: An outstanding wizard awarded the **Order of Merlin**.
- Belby choked on pheasant but was saved by Slughorn's **Anapneo** spell.
- Belby admitted tension in his family, as his dad and uncle don’t get on well.
- **McLaggen** mentioned hunting nogtails in Norfolk with **Bertie Higgs** and **Rufus Scrimgeour** (before he became Minister).
- Zabini’s mother was famously married seven times; each husband died mysteriously, leaving her wealth.

### Neville’s Turn

Neville was uncomfortable. His parents, well-known **Aurors**, had been tortured into insanity by **Bellatrix Lestrange** and some Death Eaters.

- Slughorn seemed to reserve judgment on Neville, uncertain if he inherited his parents’ flair.

### Slughorn Turns to Harry

Slughorn introduced Harry as the **“Chosen One”**.

- Recalled the **terrible night** when Lily and James Potter were killed but Harry survived.
- Mentioned rumors of Harry's extraordinary powers.
- Zabini showed skepticism.
- Slughorn spoke of the **disturbance at the Ministry** Harry was involved in.
- Slughorn praised Harry's modesty, much admired by **Dumbledore**.

### Discussion of the Prophecy

- Neville claimed **no prophecy** was heard.
- Ginny supported this, calling the **Prophet’s** stories “Made up.”
- Slughorn referenced **Gwenog Jones**, captain of the **Holyhead Harpies**, but seemed unconvinced.

## Observations and Social Dynamics

The afternoon passed with Slughorn narrating anecdotes about illustrious wizards he had taught, all proud to be in the **“Slug Club.”** Harry felt eager to leave.

- The train emerged from mist into a **red sunset**.
- Slughorn reminded everyone to change into their robes.
- Slughorn invited McLaggen, Harry, Blaise, and Ginny to visit anytime.

Neville commented, “Strange man, isn’t he?”

Ginny explained she was invited because Slughorn saw her hex **Zacharias Smith** from **Hufflepuff** who annoyed her with questions about the Ministry; Slughorn admired the hex rather than punished her.

Harry scowled at Zabini, thinking it was better to be invited for real talent or connections, not family fame.

## Harry’s Secret Plan

Harry hatched a risky plan to spy on Zabini and Malfoy:

- Zabini was going to re-enter the **Slytherin sixth-year compartment**.
- Harry planned to follow covertly with his **Invisibility Cloak**.
- The journey was nearly over, with **Hogsmeade Station** less than half an hour away.

Neville was confused; Harry whispered “Later!” and slipped after Zabini.

## In the Slytherin Compartment

The corridors were nearly empty. Everyone was changing into robes and packing.

- Harry was barely fast enough to slip into the compartment when Zabini shut the door.
- Zabini hit the sliding door on Harry’s foot in frustration.
- Harry forced it open, causing Zabini to topple into **Gregory Goyle’s** lap.
- Harry climbed into the **luggage rack**, hidden under the cloak.
- Goyle and Zabini argued, distracting others.
- Malfoy lay across seats, his head on **Pansy Parkinson’s** lap, who stroked his blond hair smugly.

### Conversation Inside the Compartment

Malfoy and Zabini talked:

- Malfoy: “So, Zabini, what did Slughorn want?”
- Zabini: Slughorn was trying to make up to well-connected people but found few.

Malfoy asked whom else Slughorn invited:

- McLaggen from Gryffindor
- Belby from Ravenclaw (called a “prat” by Pansy)
- Longbottom, Potter, and Weasley (Ginny)

Malfoy reacted strongly:

- Shocked Slughorn invited **Longbottom**.
- Puzzled what Longbottom could offer Slughorn.
- Called Potter the **“Chosen One”**.
- Dismissed Weasley’s importance.

---

**Important Characters & Terms:**

- **Slughorn** - Host and influential wizard
- **Blaise Zabini** - Slytherin, son of a famously married witch
- **Cormac McLaggen** - Gryffindor student, tied to the Ministry
- **Marcus Belby** - Nervous Ravenclaw, family tension
- **Ginny Weasley** - Gryffindor, known for Bat-Bogey Hex
- **Neville Longbottom** - Traumatized Auror’s son, Slughorn uncertain about him
- **Harry Potter** - The “Chosen One,” subject of rumors and prophecy
- **Anapneo** - A spell to clear airways
- **Order of Merlin** - Prestigious wizarding award
- **Dumbledore** - Admired mentor to Harry
- **Ministry of Magic** - Site of recent disturbances
- **Invisibility Cloak** - Magical item Harry uses for stealth
- **Hogsmeade Station** - Final stop before Hogwarts
- **Malfoy** - Slytherin antagonist
- **Gregory Goyle & Vincent Crabbe** - Malfoy’s followers
- **Pansy Parkinson** - Malfoy’s admirer

## Dialogue on the Train

**Pansy** observed **Malfoy**, noting:  
- “A lot of boys like her.”  
- Even **Blaise Zabini**, known to be hard to please, found her good-looking.  

**Zabini** replied coldly:  
- “I wouldn’t touch a filthy little blood traitor like her whatever she looked like.”  
- Pansy appeared pleased by this.  

**Malfoy** leaned back and allowed Pansy to stroke his hair, commenting on **Slughorn's** taste:  
- Perhaps Slughorn was senile.  
- His father considered Slughorn a good wizard in his day and was once a favorite of his.  
- Slughorn likely hadn’t heard Malfoy was on the train.  

**Zabini** disagreed about invitations:  
- Slughorn asked about **Nott’s** father, an old friend, but was displeased when he heard Nott was caught at the Ministry.  
- Nott did not receive an invitation, implying Slughorn’s disinterest in **Death Eaters**.  

**Malfoy** responded angrily but laughed humorlessly:  
- Dismissed Slughorn as “just some stupid teacher.”  
- Considered the possibility of not attending **Hogwarts** next year.  

**Pansy** questioned Malfoy’s plans:  
- Malfoy hinted at moving on to “bigger and better things.”  
- This caused surprise among the group, including Crabbe, Goyle, and Zabini.  

**Malfoy** revealed his thoughts on education under the **Dark Lord**:  
- His mother wants him to complete his education.  
- He doubts the importance of O.W.L.s or N.E.W.T.s when the Dark Lord takes over.  
- Success will depend on service and devotion, not qualifications.  

**Zabini** challenged him:  
- Criticized Malfoy’s youth and lack of qualifications.  

**Malfoy** retorted quietly:  
- Qualifications might be irrelevant for his intended role.  

Crabbe and Goyle looked stunned. Pansy was in awe as Malfoy pointed out Hogwarts through the window and suggested getting their robes on.  

## Harry’s Hidden Position and Discovery

Harry, hiding beneath his **Invisibility Cloak** in the luggage rack, was distracted by Malfoy’s remarks. Suddenly:  
- Goyle swung down a trunk, which hit Harry on the head.  
- Harry gasped, and Malfoy frowned looking up.  

Harry drew his wand cautiously, fearing discovery by unfriendly **Slytherins**. Malfoy ignored the noise and prepared to leave, donning a thick traveling cloak.  

The train slowed and finally stopped, allowing passengers to disembark. Goyle pushed through a crowd, followed by Crabbe and Zabini.  

**Malfoy** told **Pansy** he needed to “check something,” prompting her to leave. Now alone with Harry, Malfoy:  
- Closed the compartment blinds.  
- Bent over his trunk and opened it again.  

Harry watched, nervous about what Malfoy wanted to hide—possibly the mysterious broken object.  

Suddenly, Malfoy cast **Petrificus Totalus!**, causing Harry to be paralyzed and crash from the luggage rack to the floor. His **Invisibility Cloak** was trapped beneath him, fully revealing his body.  

Malfoy smiled triumphantly, noting:  
- Goyle’s trunk hit Harry.  
- Something white flashed after Zabini returned.  
- Harry blocked the door when Zabini came back.  

Malfoy pressed his victory, stating:  
- Harry hadn’t heard anything important.  
- Then stomped hard on Harry’s face, breaking his nose and causing blood to spurt.  

He then dragged the cloak over Harry and quietly said:  
- “I don’t reckon they’ll find you till the train’s back in London.”  
- “See you around, Potter… or not.”  

Malfoy deliberately stepped on Harry’s fingers before leaving the compartment.  

## 8. SNAPE VICTORIOUS

Harry lay helpless, blood flowing from his broken nose, trapped beneath the **Invisibility Cloak**. Although the train was noisy outside, Harry hoped no one would find him.  

He hated Malfoy more than ever, trapped like a turtle on its back while bleeding. He feared Ron and Hermione would think he had left the train alone.  

Harry tried to make noise or summon his wand with **Accio Wand!**, but failed. The distant sounds of nature and laughter from the school arrival brought no hope.  

The train lurched, and Harry rolled to his side as the engine roared and the Express began its journey to Hogwarts, with nobody aware of Harry’s presence.  

Suddenly, the cloak was removed and a voice said:  
- “Wotcher, Harry.”  

A flash of red light freed Harry from paralysis. He saw **Tonks**, holding the cloak.  

Tonks urged Harry to leave quickly, saying:  
- “Come on, we’ll jump.”  

They exited the train onto the platform as it gained speed and disappeared from view.  

The cold night air soothed Harry’s bruised nose. Tonks handed him back his cloak silently and asked:  
- “Who did it?”  

Harry bitterly replied:  
- “Draco Malfoy. Thanks for… well…”  

Tonks was unamused and offered to fix his nose with healing magic. Despite Harry’s reluctance, she cast **Episkey**, and the nose felt healed.  

Tonks instructed:  
- “You’d better put that cloak back on, and we can walk up to the school.”  

She then summoned a large silvery four-legged creature, which streaked off into the darkness.  

Harry asked about the creature, and Tonks explained:  
- “Yes, I’m sending word to the castle that I’ve got you or they’ll worry.”  

They set off toward the lane leading to Hogwarts.  

Harry inquired how Tonks had found him, and she said:  
- She noticed he hadn’t left the train and suspected he was hiding.  
- She saw the compartment blinds drawn and decided to check.  

Harry asked about her presence there:  
- Tonks is stationed in **Hogsmeade** to provide extra protection for the school.  

Harry probed whether she was alone:  
- Tonks confirmed others were stationed there, including **Proudfoot**, **Savage**, and **Dawlish**.  

Harry recognized Dawlish and asked:  
- “Dawlish, that Auror Dumbledore attacked last year?”  

Tonks affirmed.

## Arrival at Hogwarts

They trudged up the **dark, deserted lane**, following the freshly made carriage tracks. **Harry** looked sideways at **Tonks** under his cloak. Last year she had been inquisitive and jovial; now she seemed **older**, **more serious**, and **purposeful**. Harry reflected that this change might be due to what had happened at the **Ministry**.

Harry avoided consoling Tonks about **Sirius's death**, fearing the topic. They continued silently in the cold night, Tonks’s long cloak whispering behind them.

## Reaching the Hogwarts Gates

Having traveled by carriage before, Harry had never appreciated the distance between **Hogsmeade Station** and **Hogwarts**. He felt relief upon seeing the tall pillars topped with **winged boars**. Hungry and cold, he was eager to leave gloomy Tonks but found the gates **chained shut**.

- Harry tried **"Alohomora"**, but it didn’t work.
- Tonks explained the gates were bewitched by **Dumbledore** himself.
- Climbing was impossible due to **anti-intruder jinxes**.
- Security had been tightened significantly.

Tonks said someone was coming for Harry, and soon a **lantern** appeared near the castle. Harry recognized the bearer as **Severus Snape**, his loathing intensifying.

## Encounter with Snape

Snape tapped the padlock open with his wand and sneered at Harry for his **lack of school robes**. He dismissed Tonks, claiming Potter was safe.

- Snape mentioned **Hagrid** was late for the feast, so he took the message instead.
- He commented on Harry’s new **Patronus**, saying the old one was better.
- Snape shut the gates and left Tonks outside.

Harry thanked Tonks silently as he walked with Snape toward the castle, his hatred for Snape fueled by memories of Snape’s attitude toward **Sirius** and his suspicion that Snape’s remarks contributed to Sirius’s death.

## Snape’s Rebuke

Snape deducted **fifty points** from Gryffindor for Harry’s tardiness and **twenty more** for wearing Muggle clothes. He mocked Harry for making a dramatic entrance without a flying car, suggesting Harry wanted attention.

Harry stayed silent, though seething with rage. Snape's presence was a torment he wished to escape.

## Entering the Great Hall

At the castle steps, Snape forbade Harry from wearing his **Invisibility Cloak** inside. Harry marched into the **Great Hall**, decorated with **floating candles** and four long House tables.

Harry hurried to **Ron** and **Hermione** who noted his **bloody face**. Hermione used her wand to clean the dried blood with **"Tergeo!"**. Harry avoided details, wanting to appear heroic. Nearby, **Ginny**, **Neville**, **Dean**, **Seamus**, and **Nearly Headless Nick** eavesdropped.

- Harry enjoyed some food, swapped chicken and chips for puddings missed during his absence.
- Hermione agreed the Sorting Hat’s message was typical: **unite against enemies**.
- Dumbledore’s speech was anticipated after the feast.

Hagrid, though late, waved at Harry from the staff table between **Professor McGonagall** and **Professor Trelawney**. Harry felt uneasy around Trelawney, recalling her prophecy concerning Voldemort and his family’s tragedy.

**Draco Malfoy** entertained Slytherin with mocking gestures about Harry’s injured nose, fueling Harry’s anger.

## Conversation With Friends

Harry told Hermione the story was for later. Ron shared the news of others interrogating Harry about being the **"Chosen One."**

Nearly Headless Nick joked about his loyalty and the ghosts’ curiosity, though Ron mocked him for being dead.

Nick responded with offended humor and returned to his seat as **Dumbledore** stood to address the hall.

## Dumbledore’s Speech

Dumbledore greeted everyone warmly, though many noticed his **blackened right hand**, reminiscent of the night he fetched Harry from the Dursleys.

- He smiled and reassured the students not to worry.
- Welcomed **new students** and welcomed back **old students**.
- Announced another year of **magical education** ahead.

## Scene: The Great Hall Conversation

“His hand was like that when I saw him over the summer,” **Harry** whispered to **Hermione**. “I thought he’d have cured it by now, though… or **Madam Pomfrey** would’ve done.”

“It looks as if it’s **died**,” said Hermione, with a nauseated expression. “But there are some **injuries you can’t cure**… **old curses**… and there are **poisons without antidotes**…”

## Announcements at Hogwarts

“…and **Mr. Filch**, our caretaker, has asked me to say that there is a **blanket ban** on any **joke items** bought at the shop called **Weasleys’ Wizard Wheezes**.

- Those wishing to play for their House **Quidditch teams** should give their names to their **Heads of House** as usual.
- The school is also looking for new **Quidditch commentators**, who should also volunteer.

## Staff Introduction and Changes

“We are pleased to welcome a **new member of staff this year**, **Professor Slughorn**” — Slughorn stood up, his bald head gleaming in the candlelight, his big waistcoated belly casting the table into shadow — “a former colleague of mine who has agreed to resume his old post of **Potions master**.”

“Potions?” 

“Potions?” 

The word echoed all over the Hall as people wondered if they had heard right.

### Confusion Over Professor Roles

“Potions?” said **Ron** and **Hermione** together, turning to stare at Harry. “But you said—”

“**Professor Snape**, meanwhile,” said **Dumbledore**, raising his

## Neville Longbottom’s N.E.W.T. Results and Course Selection

“**Herbology, fine**,” she said. “Professor Sprout will be delighted to see you back with an ‘**Outstanding**’ O.W.L. And you qualify for **Defense Against the Dark Arts** with ‘**Exceeds Expectations**.’ But the problem is **Transfiguration**. I’m sorry, Longbottom, but an ‘**Acceptable**’ really isn’t good enough to continue to N.E.W.T. level. Just don’t think you’d be able to cope with the coursework.”

Neville hung his head. **Professor McGonagall** peered at him through her square spectacles.

“Why do you want to continue with Transfiguration, anyway? I’ve never had the impression that you particularly enjoyed it.”

Neville looked miserable and muttered something about “**my grandmother wants**.”

“Hmph,” snorted **Professor

## Facing Voldemort and Bravery

“Yes, when you were telling us what it’s like to face **Voldemort**. You said it wasn’t just memorizing a bunch of spells, you said it was just you and your brains and your guts—well, wasn’t that what **Snape** was saying? That it really comes down to being **brave** and **quick-thinking**?”

Harry was so disarmed that she had thought his words as well worth memorizing as *The Standard Book of Spells* that he did not argue.

## Quidditch and Private Lessons

### Jack Sloper’s Message

“Harry! Hey, Harry!”

Harry looked around; **Jack Sloper**, one of the **Beaters** on last year’s **Gryffindor Quidditch** team, was hurrying toward him holding a roll of parchment.

“For you,” panted Sloper. “Listen, I heard you’re the new **Captain**. When’re you holding trials?”

“I’m not sure yet,” said Harry, thinking privately that Sloper would be very lucky to get back on the team. “I’ll let you know.”

“Oh, right. I was hoping it’d be this weekend—”

But Harry was not listening; he had just recognized the thin, slanting writing on the parchment. Leaving Sloper in mid-sentence, he hurried away with **Ron** and **Hermione**, unrolling the parchment as he went.

### Dumbledore’s Letter

Dear Harry,

I would like to start our private lessons this **Saturday**. Kindly come along to my office at **8 P.M.** I hope you are enjoying your first day back at school.

Yours sincerely,  
**Albus Dumbledore**

P.S. I enjoy **Acid Pops**.

---

“He enjoys Acid Pops?” said Ron, who had read the message over Harry’s shoulder and was looking perplexed.

“It’s the **password** to get past the gargoyle outside his study,” said Harry in a low voice. “Ha! Snape’s not going to be pleased… I won’t be able to do his detention!”

## Speculating on Dumbledore’s Teachings

He, Ron, and Hermione spent the whole of break speculating on what **Dumbledore** would teach Harry. Ron thought it most likely to be spectacular **jinxes** and **hexes** of the type the **Death Eaters** would not know. Hermione said such things were illegal, and thought it much more likely that Dumbledore wanted to teach Harry advanced **Defensive magic**.

After break, she went off to **Arithmancy** while Harry and Ron returned to the common room where they grudgingly started **Snape’s homework**. This turned out to be so complex that they still had not finished when Hermione joined them for their after-lunch free period (though she considerably speeded up the process).

They had only just finished when the bell rang for the afternoon’s double **Potions** and they beat the familiar path down to the dungeon classroom that had, for so long, been Snape’s.

## N.E.W.T. Potions Class with Slughorn

### Students and Atmosphere

When they arrived in the corridor they saw that there were only a dozen people progressing to **N.E.W.T. level**. **Crabbe** and **Goyle** had evidently failed to achieve the required **O.W.L.** grade, but four **Slytherins** had made it through, including **Malfoy**. Four **Ravenclaws** were there, and one **Hufflepuff**, **Ernie Macmillan**, whom Harry liked despite his rather pompous manner.

“Harry,” Ernie said portentously, holding out his hand as Harry approached, “didn’t get a chance to speak in **Defense Against The Dark Arts** this morning. Good lesson, I thought, but Shield Charms are old hat, of course, for us old D.A. lags… And how are you, Ron—Hermione?”

Before they could say more than “fine,” the dungeon door opened and **Slughorn’s** belly preceded him out of the door. As they filed into the room, his great **walrus mustache** curved above his beaming mouth, and he greeted Harry and Zabini with particular enthusiasm.

### Potions and Classroom Setup

The dungeon was, most unusually, already full of vapors and odd smells. Harry, Ron, and Hermione sniffed interestedly as they passed large, bubbling **cauldrons**. The four Slytherins took a table together, as did the four Ravenclaws. This left Harry, Ron, and Hermione to share a table with Ernie.

They chose the one nearest a gold-colored cauldron that was emitting one of the most seductive scents Harry had ever inhaled: Somehow it reminded him simultaneously of **treacle tart**, the woody smell of a **broomstick handle**, and something flowery he thought he might have smelled at the **Burrow**.

He found that he was breathing very slowly and deeply and that the potion’s **fumes** seemed to be filling him up like drink. A great contentment stole over him; he grinned across at Ron, who grinned back lazily.

### Slughorn’s Introduction

“Now then, now then, now then,” said Slughorn, whose massive outline was quivering through the many shimmering vapors. “**Scales out**, everyone, and potion kits, and don’t forget your copies of *Advanced Potion-Making*…”

“Sir?” said Harry, raising his hand.

“Harry, m’boy?”

“I haven’t got a book or scales or anything—nor’s Ron—we didn’t realize we’d be able to do the N.E.W.T., you see—”

“Ah, yes, **Professor McGonagall** did mention… not to worry, my dear boy, not to worry at all. You can use ingredients from the store cupboard today, and I’m sure we can lend you some scales, and we’ve got a small stock of old books here, they’ll do until you can write to **Flourish and Blotts**…”

Slughorn strode over to a corner cupboard and, after a moment’s foraging, emerged with two very battered-looking copies of *Advanced Potion-Making* by **Libatius Borage**, which he gave to Harry and Ron along with two sets of **tarnished scales**.

“Now then,” said Slughorn, returning to the front of the class and inflating his already bulging chest so that the buttons on his waistcoat threatened to burst off, “I’ve prepared a few potions for you to have a look at, just out of interest, you know. These are the kind of thing you ought to be able to make after completing your N.E.W.T.s. You ought to have heard of ’em, even if you haven’t made ’em yet. Anyone tell me what this one is?”

### Identifying Potions

He indicated the cauldron nearest the Slytherin table. Harry raised himself slightly in his seat and saw what looked like plain water boiling

## Potion-Making Challenge

“So,” said **Slughorn**, suddenly brisk, “how are you to win this **fabulous prize**? Well, by turning to page ten of **Advanced Potion-making**. We have a little over an hour left to us, which should be time for you to make a decent attempt at the **Draught of Living Death**. I know it is more complex than anything you have attempted before, and I do not expect a perfect potion from anybody. The person who does best, however, will win little **Felix** here. Off you go!”

There was a scraping as everyone drew their **cauldrons** toward them and some loud clunks as people began adding weights to their **scales**, but nobody spoke. The concentration within the room was almost tangible. **Harry** saw **Malfoy** riffling feverishly through his copy of **Advanced Potion-Making**. It could not have been clearer that Malfoy really wanted that lucky day. Harry bent swiftly over the tattered book Slughorn had lent him.

To his annoyance he saw that the previous owner had scribbled all over the pages, so that the margins were as black as the printed portions. Bending low to decipher the ingredients (even here, the previous owner had made annotations and crossed things out) Harry hurried off toward the **store cupboard** to find what he needed. As he dashed back to his cauldron, he saw Malfoy cutting up **Valerian roots** as fast as he could.

Everyone kept glancing around at what the rest of the class was doing; this was both an advantage and a disadvantage of **Potions**, that it was hard to keep your work private. Within ten minutes, the whole place was full of **bluish steam**. **Hermione**, of course, seemed to have progressed furthest. Her potion already resembled the “smooth, blackcurrant-colored liquid” mentioned as the ideal halfway stage.

Having finished chopping his roots, Harry bent low over his book again. It was really very irritating, having to try and decipher the directions under all the stupid scribbles of the previous owner, who for some reason had taken issue with the order to cut up the **sopophorous bean** and had written in the alternative instruction:

**Crush with flat side of silver dagger, releases juice better than cutting.**

---

## Interaction with Slughorn and Malfoy

“Sir, I think you knew my grandfather, **Abraxas Malfoy**?”

Harry looked up; Slughorn was just passing the Slytherin table.

“Yes,” said Slughorn, without looking at Malfoy, “I was sorry to hear he had died, although of course it wasn’t unexpected, **dragon pox** at his age…”

And he walked away. Harry bent back over his cauldron, smirking. He could tell that Malfoy had expected to be treated like Harry or **Zabini**; perhaps even hoped for some preferential treatment of the type he had learned to expect from **Snape**. It looked as though Malfoy would have to rely on nothing but talent to win the bottle of **Felix Felicis**.

The **sopophorous bean** was proving very difficult to cut up. Harry turned to Hermione.

“Can I borrow your silver knife?”

She nodded impatiently, not taking her eyes off her potion, which was still deep purple, though according to the book ought to be turning a light shade of **lilac** by now.

Harry crushed his bean with the flat side of the dagger. To his astonishment, it immediately exuded so much juice he was amazed the shriveled bean could have held it all.

Hastily scooping it all into the cauldron he saw, to his surprise, that the potion immediately turned exactly the shade of **lilac** described by the textbook.

---

## Stirring the Potion

His annoyance with the previous owner vanishing on the spot, Harry now squinted at the next line of instructions. According the book, he had to **stir counterclockwise** until the potion turned clear as water. According to the addition the previous owner made, however, he ought to **add a clockwise stir after every seventh counterclockwise stir**. Could the old owner be right twice?

Harry stirred counterclockwise, held his breath, and stirred once clockwise. The effect was immediate. The potion turned **pale pink**.

“How are you doing that?” demanded Hermione, who was redfaced and whose hair was growing bushier and bushier in the fumes from her cauldron; her potion was still resolutely purple.

“Add a clockwise stir—”

“No, no, the book says counterclockwise!” she snapped.

Harry shrugged and continued what he was doing. Seven stirs counterclockwise, one clockwise, pause… seven stirs counterclockwise, one stir clockwise

## Harry's Detention and Meeting with Dumbledore

“I have arranged with **Professor Snape** that you will do your detention next Saturday instead.”

“Right,” said **Harry**, who had more pressing matters on his mind than **Snape’s detention**, and now looked around surreptitiously for some indication of what **Dumbledore** was planning to do with him this evening. The circular office looked just as it always did; the delicate silver instruments stood on spindle-legged tables, puffing smoke and whirring; portraits of previous headmasters and headmistresses dozed in their frames, and **Dumbledore’s magnificent phoenix, Fawkes**, stood on his perch behind the door, watching **Harry** with bright interest. It did not even look as though **Dumbledore** had cleared a space for dueling practice.

---

## 1. Discussion of Lessons and Information

“So, **Harry**,” said **Dumbledore**, in a businesslike voice. “You have been wondering, I am sure, what I have planned for you during these—for want of a better word—lessons?”

“Yes, sir.”

“Well, I have decided that it is time, now that you know what prompted **Lord Voldemort** to try and kill you fifteen years ago, for you to be given certain information.” There was a pause.

“You said, at the end of last term, you were going to tell me everything,” said **Harry**. It was hard to keep a note of accusation from his voice. “Sir,” he added.

“And so I did,” said **Dumbledore** placidly. “I told you everything I know. From this point forth, we shall be leaving the firm foundation of fact and journeying together through the murky marshes of memory into thickets of wildest guesswork. From here on in, **Harry**, I may be as woefully wrong as **Humphrey Belcher**, who believed the time was ripe for a cheese cauldron.”

“But you think you’re right?” said **Harry**.

“Naturally I do, but as I have already proven to you, I make mistakes like the next man. In fact, being—forgive me—rather cleverer than most men, my mistakes tend to be correspondingly huger.”

“Sir,” said **Harry** tentatively, “does what you’re going to tell me have anything to do with the **prophecy**? Will it help me… survive?”

“It has a very great deal to do with the **prophecy**,” said **Dumbledore**, as casually as if **Harry** had asked him about the next day's weather, “and I certainly hope that it will

## Dialogue at the Gaunt House

“I don’t doubt it, if your son’s been let loose on them,” said **Ogden**. “Perhaps we could continue this discussion inside?”

“Inside?”

“Yes, **Mr. Gaunt**. I’ve already told you. I’m here about **Morfin**. We sent an owl—”

“I’ve no use for owls,” said **Gaunt**. “I don’t open letters.”

“Then you can hardly complain that you get no warning of visitors,” said **Ogden** tartly. “I am here following a serious breach of **Wizarding law**, which occurred here in the early hours of this morning—”

“All right, all right, all right!” bellowed **Gaunt**. “Come in the bleeding house, then, and much good it’ll do you!”

## Inside the Gaunt House

The house seemed to contain three tiny rooms. Two doors led off the main room, which served as kitchen and living room combined. **Morfin** was sitting in a filthy armchair beside the smoking fire, twisting a **live adder** between his thick fingers and crooning softly at it in **Parseltongue**:

**Hissy, hissy, little snakey,**

**Slither on the floor**

**You be good to Morfin**

**Or he’ll nail you to the door.**

There was a scuffling noise in the corner beside the open window, and **Harry** realized that there was somebody else in the room: a girl whose **ragged gray dress** was the exact color of the dirty stone wall behind her. She was standing beside a steaming pot on a grimy black stove, fiddling with the shelf of squalid-looking pots and pans above it.

Her hair was lank and dull and she had a plain, pale, rather heavy face. Her eyes, like her brother’s, stared in opposite directions. She looked a little cleaner than the two men, but Harry thought he had never seen a more defeated-looking person.

“M’daughter, **Merope**,” said **Gaunt** grudgingly, as **Ogden** looked inquiringly toward her.

“Good morning,” said **Ogden**.

She did not answer, but with a frightened glance at her father turned her back on the room and continued shifting the pots on the shelf behind her.

## Ogden Confronts Gaunt About Magic Usage

“Well, Mr. Gaunt,” said **Ogden**, “to get straight to the point, we have reason to believe that your son, **Morfin**, performed **magic** in front of a **Muggle** late last night.”

There was a deafening clang. **Merope** had dropped one of the pots.

“Pick it up!” **Gaunt** bellowed at her. “That’s it, grub on the floor like some filthy Muggle, what’s your **wand** for, you useless sack of muck?”

“Mr. Gaunt, please!” said **Ogden** in a shocked voice, as **Merope**, who had already picked up the pot, flushed blotchily scarlet, lost her grip on the pot again, drew her wand shakily from her pocket, pointed it at the pot, and muttered a hasty, inaudible **spell** that caused the pot to shoot across the floor, hit the opposite wall, and crack in two.

**Morfin** let out a mad cackle of laughter. **Gaunt** screamed, “Mend it, you pointless lump, mend it!”

**Merope** stumbled across the room, but before she had time to raise her wand, **Ogden** lifted his own and said firmly, "**Reparo.**" The pot mended itself instantly.

## Gaunt’s Family Pride and Contempt

**Gaunt** looked as though he was going to shout at **Ogden**, but seemed to think better of it. Instead, he jeered at his daughter:

“Lucky the nice man from the Ministry’s here, isn’t it? Perhaps he’ll take you off my hands, perhaps he doesn’t mind dirty **Squibs**…”

Without looking at anybody or thanking **Ogden**, **Merope** returned the pot trembling to its shelf and stood quite still, as though wishing to vanish.

“Mr. Gaunt,” **Ogden** began again, “as I’ve said: the reason for my visit—”

“I heard you the first time!” snapped **Gaunt**. “And so what? Morfin gave a Muggle a bit of what was coming to him—what about it, then?”

“Morfin has broken **Wizarding law**,” said **Ogden** sternly.

“‘Morfin has broken Wizarding law.’” **Gaunt** imitated **Ogden’s** voice mockingly. **Morfin** cackled again. “He taught a filthy Muggle a lesson, that’s illegal now, is it?”

“Yes,” said **Ogden**. “I’m afraid it is.”

## The Ministry Summons

He pulled from an inside pocket a small scroll of parchment and unrolled it.

“What’s that, then, his sentence?” said **Gaunt**, voice rising angrily.

“It is a **summons** to the Ministry for a **hearing**—”

“Summons! Summons? Who do you think you are, summoning my son anywhere?”

“I’m Head of the **Magical Law Enforcement Squad**,” said **Ogden**.

“And you think we’re scum, do you?” screamed **Gaunt**, advancing on **Ogden** with a dirty yellow-nailed finger pointing at his chest. “Scum who’ll come running when the Ministry tells ’em to? Do you know who you’re talking to, you filthy little **Mudblood**, do you?”

“I was under the impression that I was speaking to Mr. Gaunt,” said **Ogden**, wary but standing his ground.

“That’s right!” roared **Gaunt**, showing an ugly, black-stoned **ring** on his middle finger, waving it before **Ogden’s** eyes.

“See this? Know where it came from? Centuries it’s been in our family, pure-blood all the way! Know how much I’ve been offered for this, with the **Peverell coat of arms** engraved on the stone?”

“I’ve really no idea,” said **Ogden**, blinking as the ring sailed within an inch of his nose, “and it’s quite beside the point, Mr. Gaunt. Your son has committed—”

## Violence Breaks Out

With a howl of rage, **Gaunt** ran toward his daughter. For a split second Harry thought he was going to throttle her as his hand flew to her throat; next moment, he was dragging her toward **Ogden** by a gold chain around her neck.

“See this?” he bellowed at **Ogden**, shaking a heavy gold **locket** at him, while **Merope** spluttered and gasped for breath.

“**Slytherin’s!**” yelled **Gaunt**. “**Salazar Slytherin’s!** We’re his last living descendants, what do you say to that, eh?”

“Mr. Gaunt, your daughter!” said **Ogden** in alarm, but **Gaunt** had already released **Merope**; she staggered back to her corner, massaging her neck and gulping for air.

“So!” said **Gaunt** triumphantly. “Don’t you go talking to us as if we’re dirt on your shoes! Generations of **pure-bloods**, wizards all—more than you can say, I don’t doubt!”

He spat

## 10. Voldemort’s Family History

“Oh, she survived,” said **Dumbledore**, reseating himself behind his desk and indicating that **Harry** should sit down too. “**Ogden** Apparated back to the Ministry and returned with reinforcements within fifteen minutes. **Morfin** and his father attempted to fight, but both were overpowered, removed from the cottage, and subsequently convicted by the **Wizengamot**. Morfin, who already had a record of **Muggle attacks**, was sentenced to three years in **Azkaban**. **Marvolo**, who had injured several Ministry employees in addition to Ogden, received six months.”

“**Marvolo**?” Harry repeated wonderingly.

“That’s right,” said Dumbledore, smiling in approval. “I am glad to see you’re keeping up.”

“That old man was—?”

“**Voldemort’s grandfather,** yes,” said Dumbledore. “Marvolo, his son, Morfin, and his daughter, **Merope**, were the last of the **Gaunts**, a very ancient Wizarding family noted for a vein of instability and violence that flourished through the generations due to their habit of marrying their own cousins. Lack of sense coupled with a great liking for grandeur meant that the family gold was squandered several generations before Marvolo was born. He, as you saw, was left in squalor and poverty, with a very nasty temper, a fantastic amount of arrogance and pride, and a couple of family heirlooms that he treasured just as much as his son, and rather more than his daughter.”

“So Merope,” said Harry, leaning forward in his chair and staring at Dumbledore, “so Merope was… Sir, does that mean she was… **Voldemort’s mother**?”

“It does,” said Dumbledore. “And it so happens that we also had a glimpse of **Voldemort’s father**. I wonder whether you noticed?”

“The Muggle Morfin attacked? The man on the horse?”

“Very good indeed,” said Dumbledore, beaming. “Yes, that was **Tom Riddle senior**, the handsome Muggle who used to go riding past the Gaunt cottage and for whom Merope Gaunt cherished a secret, burning passion.”

“And they ended up married?” Harry said in disbelief, unable to imagine two people less likely to fall in love.

“I think you are forgetting,” said Dumbledore, “that Merope was a **witch**. I do not believe that her magical powers appeared to their best advantage when she was being terrorized by her father. Once Marvolo and Morfin were safely in Azkaban, once she was alone and free for the first time in her life, then, I am sure, she was able to give full rein to her abilities and to plot her escape from the desperate life she had led for eighteen years.

“Can you not think of any measure Merope could have taken to make Tom Riddle forget his Muggle companion, and fall in love with her instead?”

“The **Imperius Curse**?” Harry suggested. “Or a **love potion**?”

“Very good. Personally, I am inclined to think that she used a **love potion**. I am sure it would have seemed more romantic to her, and I do not think it would have been very difficult, some hot day, when Riddle was riding alone, to persuade him to take a drink of water. In any case, within a few months of the scene we have just witnessed, the village of **Little Hangleton** enjoyed a tremendous scandal. You can imagine the gossip it caused when the squire’s son ran off with the tramp’s daughter, Merope.”

“But the villagers’ shock was nothing to **Marvolo’s**. He returned from Azkaban, expecting to find his daughter dutifully awaiting his return with a hot meal ready on his table. Instead, he found a clear inch of dust and her note of farewell, explaining what she had done.”

“From all that I have been able to discover, he never mentioned her name or existence from that time forth. The shock of her desertion may have contributed to his early death—or perhaps he had simply never learned to feed himself. Azkaban had greatly weakened Marvolo, and he did not live to see Morfin return to the cottage.”

“And Merope? She… she died, didn’t she? Wasn’t Voldemort brought up in an orphanage?”

“Yes, indeed,” said Dumbledore. “We must do a certain amount of guessing here, although I do not think it is difficult to deduce what happened. You see, within a few months of their runaway marriage, Tom Riddle reappeared at the manor house in Little Hangleton without his wife. The rumor flew around the neighborhood that he was talking of being ‘hoodwinked’ and ‘taken in.’ What he meant, I am sure, is that he had been under an enchantment that had now lifted, though I daresay he did not dare use those precise words for fear of being thought insane. When they heard what he was saying, however, the villagers guessed that Merope had lied to Tom Riddle, pretending that she was going to have his baby, and that he had married her for this reason.”

“But she did have his baby.”

“But not until a year after they were married. Tom Riddle left her while she was still pregnant.”

“What went wrong?” asked Harry. “Why did the love potion stop working?”

“Again, this is guesswork,” said Dumbledore, “but I believe that Merope, who was deeply in love with her husband, could not bear to continue enslaving him by magical means. I believe that she made the choice to stop giving him the potion. Perhaps, besotted as she was, she had convinced herself that he would by now have fallen in love with her in return. Perhaps she thought he would stay for the baby’s sake. If so, she was wrong on both counts. He left her, never saw her again, and never troubled to discover what became of his son.”

The sky outside was inky black and the lamps in Dumbledore’s office seemed to glow more brightly than before.

“I think that will do for tonight, Harry,” said Dumbledore after a moment or two.

“Yes, sir,” said Harry.

He got to his feet, but did not leave.

“Sir… is it important to know all this about Voldemort’s past?”

“Very important, I think,” said Dumbledore.

“And it… it’s got something to do with the prophecy?”

“It has everything to do with the prophecy.”

“Right,” said Harry, a little confused, but reassured all the same.

He turned to go, then another question occurred to him, and he turned back again. “Sir, am I allowed to tell Ron and Hermione everything you’ve told me?”

Dumbledore considered him for a moment, then said, “Yes, I think **Mr. Weasley** and **Miss Granger** have proved themselves trustworthy. But Harry, I am going to ask you to ask them not to repeat any of this to anybody else. It would not be a good idea if word got around how much I know, or suspect, about Lord Voldemort’s secrets.”

“No, sir, I’ll make sure it’s just Ron and Hermione. Good night.”

He turned away again, and was almost at the door when he saw it. Sitting on one of the little spindle-legged tables that supported so many frail-looking silver instruments, was an ugly gold ring set with a large, cracked, black stone.

“Sir,” said Harry, staring at it. “That ring—”

“Yes?” said Dumbledore.

“You were wearing it when we visited **Professor Slughorn** that night.”

“So I was,” Dumbledore agreed.

“But isn’t it… sir, isn’t it the same ring **Marvolo Gaunt** showed Ogden?”

Dumbledore bowed his head. “The very same.”

“But how come—? Have you always had it?”

“No, I acquired it very recently,” said Dumbledore. “A few days before I came to fetch you from your aunt and uncle’s, in fact.”

“That would be around the time you injured your hand, then, sir?”

“Around that time, yes, Harry.”

Harry hesitated. Dumbledore was smiling.

“Sir, how exactly—?”

“Too late, Harry! You shall hear the story another time. Good night.”

“Good night, sir.”


## 11. Hermione’s Helping Hand

As Hermione had predicted, the sixth years’ free periods were not the hours of blissful relaxation Ron had anticipated, but times in which to attempt to keep up with the vast amount of **homework** they were being set. Not only were they studying as though they had exams every day, but the lessons themselves had become more demanding than ever before. Harry barely understood half of what **Professor McGonagall** said to them these days; even Hermione had had to ask her to repeat instructions once or twice. Incredibly, and to Hermione’s increasing resentment, Harry’s best subject had suddenly become **Potions**, thanks to the **Half-Blood Prince**.

Non-verbal spells were now expected, not only in **Defense Against the Dark Arts**, but in **Charms** and **Transfiguration** too. Harry frequently looked over at his classmates in the common room or at mealtimes to see them purple in the face and straining as though they had overdosed on **U-No-Poo**; but he knew that they were really struggling to make spells work without saying incantations aloud. It was a relief to get outside into the **greenhouses**; they were dealing with more dangerous plants than ever in **Herbology**, but at least they were still allowed to swear loudly if the **Venomous Tentacula** seized them unexpectedly from behind.

One result of their enormous workload and the frantic hours of practicing non-verbal spells was that Harry, Ron, and Hermione had so far been unable to find time to go and visit **Hagrid**. He had stopped coming to meals at the staff table, an ominous sign, and on the few occasions when they had passed him in the corridors or out in the grounds, he had mysteriously failed to notice them or hear their greetings.

“We’ve got to go and explain,” said Hermione, looking up at Hagrid’s huge empty chair at the staff table the following Saturday at breakfast.

“We’ve got **Quidditch tryouts** this morning!” said Ron. “And we’re supposed to be practicing that **Aguamenti Charm** from Flitwick! Anyway, explain what? How are we going to tell him we hated his stupid subject?”

“We didn’t hate it!” said Hermione.

“Speak for yourself, I haven’t forgotten the **skrewts**,” said Ron darkly. “And I’m telling you now, we’ve had a narrow escape. You didn’t hear him going on about his gormless brother—we’d have been teaching **Grawp** how to tie his shoelaces if we’d stayed.”

“I hate not talking to Hagrid,” said Hermione, looking upset.

“We’ll go down after Quidditch,” Harry assured her. He too was missing Hagrid, although like Ron he thought that they were better off without Grawp in their lives. “But trials might take all morning, the number of people who have applied.” He felt slightly nervous at confronting the first hurdle of his **Captaincy**. “I dunno why the team’s this popular all of a sudden.”

“Oh, come on, Harry,” said Hermione, suddenly impatient. “It’s not Quidditch that’s popular, it’s you! You’ve never been more interesting, and frankly, you’ve never been more fanciable.”

Ron gagged on a large piece of kipper. Hermione spared him one look of disdain before turning back to Harry.

“Everyone knows you’ve been telling the truth now, don’t they? The whole **Wizarding world** has had to admit that you were right about Voldemort being back and that you really have fought him twice in the last two years and escaped both times. And now they’re calling you **‘the Chosen One’**—well, come on, can’t you see why people are fascinated by you?”

Harry was finding the Great Hall very hot all of a sudden, even though the ceiling still looked cold and rainy.

“And you’ve been through all that persecution from the Ministry when they were trying to make out you were unstable and a liar. You can still see the marks on the back of your hand where that evil woman made you write with your own blood, but you stuck to your story anyway…”

“You can still see where those brains got hold of me in the Ministry, look,” said Ron, shaking back his sleeves.

“And it doesn’t hurt that you’ve grown about a foot over the summer either,” Hermione finished, ignoring Ron.

“I’m tall,” said Ron inconsequentially.

## Post Arrival and Mail

The **post owls** arrived, swooping down through **rain-flecked windows**, scattering everyone with droplets of water. Most people were receiving **more post than usual**; anxious parents were keen to hear from their children and to reassure them that all was well at home.
